坐客三千人,zuo'ke'san'qian'ren
坐客是瑶林,zuo'ke'shi'yao'lin
坐客同心满,zuo'ke'tong'xin'man
座客无俗心,zuo'ke'wu'su'xin
坐窥烟景穷,zuo'kui'yan'jing'qiong
昨来谁是伴,zuo'lai'shui'shi'ban
坐蓝高士去,zuo'lan'gao'shi'qu
作吏清无比,zuo'li'qing'wu'bi
作礼月光面,zuo'li'yue'guang'mian
坐领图书见督邮,zuo'ling'tu'shu'jian'du'you
昨满今渐稀,zuo'man'jin'jian'xi
坐鸣松下琴,zuo'ming'song'xia'qin
佐幕临戎旌旆间,zuo'mu'lin'rong'jing'pei'jian
座纳薰风细,zuo'na'xun'feng'xi
坐起唯从心,zuo'qi'wei'cong'xin
昨日空馀旌节还,zuo'ri'kong'yu'jing'jie'hai
昨日临川谢病还,zuo'ri'lin'chuan'xie'bing'hai
昨日偷闲看花了,zuo'ri'tou'xian'kan'hua'le
昨日一封书,zuo'ri'yi'feng'shu
昨日又隳官,zuo'ri'you'hui'guan
作瑞旌君德,zuo'rui'jing'jun'de
坐使吏相勉,zuo'shi'li'xiang'mian
坐使年病侵,zuo'shi'nian'bing'qin
作诗通小雅,zuo'shi'tong'xiao'ya
左手低,zuo'shou'di
作为公室,zuo'wei'gong'shi
坐惜年光变,zuo'xi'nian'guang'bian
坐想征人两头别,zuo'xiang'zheng'ren'liang'tou'bie
昨宵西窗梦,zuo'xiao'xi'chuang'meng
昨夜梦琼枝,zuo'ye'meng'qiong'zhi
昨夜秋风今夜雨,zuo'ye'qiu'feng'jin'ye'yu
昨夜鸳鸯梦,zuo'ye'yuan'yang'meng
昨夜月明湘浦宿,zuo'ye'yue'ming'xiang'pu'su
坐忆晓山明,zuo'yi'xiao'shan'ming
左右八貂斜,zuo'you'ba'diao'xie
左右长松列,zuo'you'chang'song'lie
左右二菩萨,zuo'you'er'pu'sa
左右皆灵娥,zuo'you'jie'ling'e
左右尽图书,zuo'you'jin'tu'shu
座右千年荫古松,zuo'you'qian'nian'yin'gu'song
作镇江山雄,zuo'zhen'jiang'shan'xiong
座中灯泛酒,zuo'zhong'deng'fan'jiu
坐中孤烛暗,zuo'zhong'gu'zhu'an
座中流泪听商声,zuo'zhong'liu'lei'ting'shang'sheng
座中琼玉润,zuo'zhong'qiong'yu'run
座中为我奏此曲,zuo'zhong'wei'wo'zou'ci'qu
